I really loved this place! It is huge with a great variety of cool stuff. From the street it appears to be a lil shop in Cambria. However, It is far from little. There is an upstairs and a downstairs. There prices are very reasonable. I have visited another shop like this in Cambria. The prices were simply rediculous unless you have an abundance of money to spend.I was really impressed with the whole place. The staff was super friendly and helpful. If you find yourself in Cambria, I would recommend a visit too Antiques on Main.</text>

<user_name>Auru Mai</user_name>< time>
1548972649108<//time>
<rate>1</rate>< review>
I've frequented this Burger King for a while since it's extremely close to where I live, but the terrible service makes the trip to another location worth it.  Almost every time I come here, I regret thinking that the short drive will result in a more convenient trip.

If you show up at the opening time posted on their door, most often they'll turn you away giving some excuse like "the broiler isn't ready" or "the system is down" (they usually freeze up if you ask them what's wrong with 'the system').  I've worked in fast food before and I've seen my fair share of lazy workers who will knowingly turn customers away because they came at an inconvenient time.  This location is either full of lazy workers who would prefer not to multitask during the opening part of the shift, or who can't be bothered to manage their time in such a way that they can actually start serving customers when they open.

I've been here maybe 15 times during hours where they weren't turning everyone away in the last year.  Literally almost every single one of those times, I was asked to wait in the parking lot (to avoid their timer showing that they take forever to complete each order), even in spite of my orders hardly ever consisting of more than 1 or 2 items.  The wait usually takes forever, and the customer service is horrendous when they eventually come to bring the food out.  There's no eye contact, no smile, no regard for their paying customers.

Go ahead and try to order something within the first 30 minutes of them opening.  You'll be turned away.  And if by some chance you're not, you'll probably be asked to wait in the parking lot regardless of how small your order is.  These people take absolutely no pride in their work.</review>

< Review>
The suit selection is great, the service is too. I bought a great wool suit for $240.  The problem came with tailoring, Gloria helped by putting pins in the sleeves and pants marking where to take things in. Unfortunately, I didn't realize the tailor would not extend those lines all the way up.  As a result I ended up with awkward-looking tapered sleeves, on a formal business suit!  When I complained, a very nice gentleman explained that was the new look, I was incredulous but it was late and I just took the suit and left. Did some research looked at pictures on line, no, that is not the new thing.  Narrow sleeves are meant to be narrow all the way up, so they make a straight line.  I didn't think they'd get it right on a second try, so I didn't go back to try to get them to fix it...  Bottom line: Do buy your suit there, don't get it tailored there.  Go see John the Tailor Man in Gardena for your fitting needs.<//Review>

Twin's Cities is a great SOCIAL GROUP.  But, to call it a true BIBLICAL CHURCH...No way and here is way.

Like many "MEGA CHURCHES", and the 5 weak/nonspiritual churches (out of 7) mentioned in the book of Rev, they are more of a TOOL OF SATAN, than they are obeying Matt 22:37-39, and Matt 28, when it comes to "The Great Commission". And you will see why as you read along. Satan and his minions do not care how the LEAD people to HELL....juts so long as they get there. The bible also says, "he comes as an angel of light and counterfeits all that is of God"....2 Cor 11"14. The book I'm working on "What God Desires Of A Healthy Church...Getting Back To The Basics" will touch on the subject of LEGALISTIC church and LIBERAL ones like Twins Cities and show the fallacies on both EXTREMES, and get Christians mindset back on BALANCE and their focus back on GOD and OTHERS, and run the church like a HOSPITAL (like Jesus said) and not a BUSINESS!!!...Listed are the reasons why Twin Cities church is NOT a healthy one...I didn't say "perfect" I said healthy...big difference...For I was in one for 8 years as a new believer 25+ years ago, so I know what one looks like....:)

1) 8,000 members, and you add up all the other mega churches and they too are in the thousands. One problem, Gods word says only, "A FEW WILL ENTER IN THE KINGDOM OF GOD, for NARROW is the way and WIDE is the road to destruction." Matt 7:13-14. Jesus also said, "YOU MUST BE BORN AGAIN TO SEE THE KINGDOM OF GOD"....Born of the spirit, one must have a spiritual REBIRTH. After attending TC, many social groups for help during a divorce, I noticed that many there were NOT SAVED, and who admitted to not being BORN AGAIN, (most had no idea what that meant) therefore they were "Christian" by name only.  Like most churches, it is a place to meet others of like mind....Thing is a TRUE believer will have NOTHING IN COMMON with these people....for they are "TARES" among the "WHEAT"...They are "WOLVES" among the "SHEEP". And from I know wolves EAT sheep.

2) The do not use a BIBLE to preach or teach out of and insist you too read out of a PARAPHRASE (man's opinion of what something says) instead of the living, inspired word of God...doesn't have to be KJ, but at least not a paraphrase bible (look it up to see what I mean) That leaves them with THEIR INTERPRETATION, not God's. That is another point I was shocked how BIBLE ILLITERATE, every one was especially the leaders...wow!...The next one might explain why....

Jack in the box was and remains one of my more favorite fast food chains for quick, hot and tasty fresh grubb.
But as with any such establishment in the last 15 years or so, you "NEVER KNOW WHAT YOU ARE GOING TO GET!"
That's totally ok when it comes to "Auntie May's" Christmas bonbons assortement of the "third kind"!
Uncertanty of quality, freshness of the product and the process requirement necessity achieved, shouldn't be something anyone, on their meal breaks or quick grab missions, may it be for indoor food purchase, with family in tow, or just as an individual at the drive through.
But it varies from place to place, unfortunately! I've had great experiences at one place, and not so satisfying ones at others. Or even changes in food quality and taste at the same establishment on a different day.
But overall still within acceptable range. 75% satisfaction overall to my observations!
I'll be visiting again though!!!
This particular Jack in the Box is one of the better ones!!!< /Text>
